		        });

  <script language="javascript">
   function submithotkeywordsearch(obj){
			searchtype(1, '');
			document.getElementById("searchform").elements["srchtxt"].value = obj.innerHTML;
			ga_trackEvent(null,'Homepage Hot Keyword',obj.innerHTML);
			document.getElementById("searchform").setAttribute("target", "_blank");
			document.getElementById("searchform").submit();
		}

		function showSearchMenu(){
			document.getElementById("search-box-menu").style.display = "block";
		}

		function hideSearchMenu(){
			document.getElementById("search-box-menu").style.display = "none";
		}

		function changeSearchAction(searchengine){
			document.searchform.srcheng.value = searchengine;
			document.searchform.target = '_self';
			if(searchengine==1){
				document.searchform.action = 'search.php';
			}else if(searchengine==2){ //advance search
				window.location = 'search.php';
			}
		}

		function searchtype(id, txt) {
			document.getElementById('search-box-menu').style.display = 'none';
			document.getElementById('current-search-item').innerHTML = txt;
			changeSearchAction(id);
		}

		function checkSrchtxt(txt){
			var srcheng = document.searchform.srcheng.value;
			if(srcheng!=2 && trim(txt.value)==''){
				alert('');
				txt.focus();
				return false;
			}
			changeSearchAction(srcheng);
			return true;
		}
  </script>

                }
            })

            $$('body').on('mouseleave', '#hot-live-main-box', function () {
                mouseState = false
                clearInterval(autoChange);
                HotLiveBoxHide();
            })

            $$('body').on('click', '#hot-live-scroll-left', function () {
                disableScroll = true;
                if (hotlive_page > 0) {
                    hotlive_page -= 1;
                    switchPage(hotlive_page)
                }
            });

            $$('body').on('click', '#hot-live-scroll-right',function () {
                disableScroll = true;
                nextPage();
            });


            $$('body').on({
                mouseenter: function(){
                    hover()
                },
                mouseleave: function(){
                    hoverLeave()
                }
            }, '#hot-live-scroll-left, #hot-live-scroll-right');

			        });

        function hover() {
            clearInterval(autoChange);
        }

        function hoverLeave() {
            clearInterval(autoChange);
            if (mouseState && !disableScroll)
                autoChange = setInterval(nextPage, timeInterval);
        }

        function switchPage(hotlive_page) {
            $$('#hot-live-box').animate({scrollLeft: 898 * hotlive_page}, 200);
            hotlive_trackEvent(hotlive_page);
            show_hotlive_paging_btn(hotlive_page);
        }

        function nextPage() {
            if (hotlive_page < getShowPage() - 1) {
                hotlive_page += 1;
                switchPage(hotlive_page)
            } else if (hotlive_page === getShowPage() - 1) {
                hotlive_page = 0;
                switchPage(hotlive_page)
            }
        }

        function show_hotlive_paging_btn(func_page) {
            if (getShowPage() <= 1) {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
                return
            }
            if (func_page == 0) {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'block');
            } else if (func_page == getShowPage() - 1) {

                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'block');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
            } else {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'block');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'block');
            }
        }

        function hotlive_trackEvent(page) {
            if (is_hotlive_array[page]) {
                return;
            }
            if (typeof dataLayer != "undefined") {
                dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'HotliveEvent',
                    'eventPage': (page + 2)
                });
            }
            is_hotlive_array[page] = true;
        }

        function HotLiveBoxHide() {
            if (live_timer_in) {
                clearTimeout(live_timer_in);
            }
            live_timer_out = setTimeout(function () {
                HotLiveBoxHideFunction();
            }, 300)
        }

        function HotLiveBoxShow() {
            if (live_timer_out) {
                clearTimeout(live_timer_out);
            }

            live_timer_in = setTimeout(function () {
                HotLiveBoxShowFunction();
            }, 300)
        }

        function HotLiveBoxHideFunction() {
            //clearTimeout(live_timer);
            $$('#hot-live-box').stop();
            //$$('#hot-live-box').animate({width:'242px'}, 500);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box').animate({width: '242px'}, 300);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').css('display', 'block');
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').animate({opacity: 100}, 300);


            $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
            $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
        }

        function HotLiveBoxShowFunction() {
            $$('#hot-live-box').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-box').animate({width: '898px'}, 100);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box').animate({width: '898px'}, 300);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').animate({opacity: 0}, 300, function () {
                $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').css('display', 'none');
                ga_trackEvent('', 'Homepage Live Topics', 'open');
                hotlive_trackEvent(hotlive_page);
                // add fire counter for abtest21 hotlive expand event
                window.firehlexpanded = true;
            });

            show_hotlive_paging_btn(hotlive_page);
            //$$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display','block');
            //$$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display','block');
        }

        function getShowPage() {
            const page = $$("input[name='showPageTmp']").val()
            if (!!page) {
                return parseInt(page)
            }
            return 20        }

        function hotliveLoaded() {
            abtest21_trackingVar = JSON.parse($$("input[name='trackingVarTmp']").val())
            if (typeof dataLayer != "undefined") {
                dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'HotliveSwitchTabEvent',
                    'eventPage': (1)
                });
            }
            HotLiveBoxShow()
            hotlive_page = 0;
            is_hotlive_array = {};
            autoChange = null;
            mouseState = true;
            disableScroll = false;
            loading = false;
            autoChange = setInterval(nextPage, timeInterval);
        }
     </script>

      </div>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       // quick link button
            $$(function () {
                var timer;
                $$("#scTab").on('click', function () {
                    if ($$("#sc").is(':hidden')) {
                        setcookie('cdb_quicklink_state', 1, 86400, '/', 'discuss.com.hk');  // it will open, change state to 1
                    } else {
                        setcookie('cdb_quicklink_state', 0, 86400, '/', 'discuss.com.hk');
                    }
                    $$("#sc").slideToggle();
                });
                $$("#qmark_icon").hover(function () {
                    clearTimeout(timer);
                    timer = setTimeout(function () {
                        $$("#qmark_content").show(0);
                    }, 500)
                }, function () {
                    clearTimeout(timer);
                    $$("#qmark_content").hide(0);
                })
            })
      </script>
